	"XXOXOO..." -> "XXOXOOX..";
	"XXOXOO..." -> "XXOXOO..X";
	"XXOXOO..." -> "XXOXOO.X.";
	"XXOXOO.OX" -> "XXOXOOXOX";
	"XXOXOX.OO" -> "XXOXOXXOO";
	"XXOXXOOO." -> "XXOXXOOOX";
}
